 co / xorkgne1vd Sarangarh assembly seat of Chhattisgarh is a reserved seat for the Scheduled Castes

 sarangarh kii siyaasi itihaas kii baat kii jaae to kabhi yahaan kii raajnneeti girivilas pales se sanchalit hoti thi
 The times have changed and the situation has changed, the Raj family has now distanced themselves from politics
 isi kaa nateeja he ki ab unki dakhsandaji najar nahin aati
 Sarangarh was once called the Congress stronghold, but a period also came when the BSP managed to hold a strong hold here
 basapa ke kaamada jolhe ne 1998 or 2003 main is seat par jeet hasil karke ise party kaa majboot durg bana diya tha
 In 2008, Congress candidate Padma Manhar broke this myth by winning elections in Sarangarh, but in 2013 BJP wrested this seat from Congress
 2013 ke nateezeybijapi ke kerabai manahar ko 81971 vot mili the
 Padma Ghanshyan Manhar of Congress got 66127 votes
 2008 ke nattijecongress ke padma ghanshyaan manahar ko 61659 vot mili the
 bjp's Shamsher Singh received 50814 votes
 2003 ke parenambaspa ke kaamada jolhe ko 32577 vot mili the
 bjp's Shyam Sundar received 24419 votes
 chhattisgarh ke sameekarnabta den ki chhattisgarh main kul 90 vidhansabha siten hai
 The state currently has a total of 11 Lok Sabha and 5 Rajya Sabha seats
 chhattisgarh main kul 27 jile hai
 a total of 51 seats in the state are reserved for general, 10 seats for SC and 29 seats for ST
 raman kii hetric2013 main vidhansabha chunaav ke nattejey 8 disambar ko ghoshit kiye gaye the
 Among them, the Bharatiya Janata Party formed the government by defeating the Congress for the third consecutive time in the state
 raman singh kii aguwai main bijepi ko 2013 main kul 49 vidhansabha siton par jeet mili thi

 jabaki 2 siten anya ke naam gai thim

 karthik shukla paksh dwitiya ko bhratridvitiya yaa yamadvitiya ke rup main manaane kii parampara he

 is din yamuna main snaan, dipadaan aadi kaa mahatv he
 On this day, sisters worship Yama and fast for the long life of the brothers
 kaha jaataa he ki jo bhai is din apni bahan se sneh or prasannataa se miltaa he, uske ghar bhojan karata he, use yama ke bhay se mukti milti he
